class="profile-section">\n                    <h2 class="profile-section-title">Biography</h2>\n                    <p>Cody Garrett Runnels Rhodes was born in Marietta, Georgia on June 30, 1985. He is the son of WWE Hall of Famer Dusty Rhodes and the half-brother of Dustin Rhodes (formerly known as Goldust in WWE).</p>\n                    <p>Cody began his wrestling career in 2006 in Ohio Valley Wrestling (OVW), WWE\'s developmental territory at the time. He made his main roster debut in 2007 and has since become one of the most accomplished wrestlers in the industry.</p>\n                    <p>After leaving WWE in 2016, Rhodes became one of the most influential figures in professional wrestling, competing in promotions like Ring of Honor, New Japan Pro Wrestling, and helping to found All Elite Wrestling (AEW) where he served as an Executive Vice President.</p>\n                    <p>In 2022, Rhodes made a shocking return to WWE at WrestleMania 38, establishing himself as one of the company\'s top stars. His journey culminated at WrestleMania XL in 2024, where he defeated Roman Reigns to win the Undisputed WWE Championship, fulfilling his family\'s legacy.</p>\n                    <p>Currently, Rhodes is in his second reign as WWE Champion after recapturing the title at SummerSlam 2025. He is recognized as one of the top stars in WWE and continues to be one of the most popular superstars on the roster.</p>\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="profile-section">\n superstarCards = document.querySelectorAll(\'.superstar-card\');\n            \n            filterOptions.forEach(option => {\n                option.addEventListener(\'click\', function() {\n                    // Remove active class from all options\n                    filterOptions.forEach(opt => opt.classList.remove(\'active\'));\n                    \n                    // Add active class to clicked option\n                    this.classList.add(\'active\');\n                    \n                    const filter = this.dataset.filter;\n                    \n                    // \'block\';\n                        } else if (filter === \'champions\') {\n                            if (card.dataset.champion === \'true\') {\n                                card.style.display = \'block\';\n                            } else {\n                                card.style.display = \'none\';\n                            }\n                        } else if (filter === \'men\' || filter === \'women\') {\n                            if (card.dataset.gender === filter) {\n                                card.style.display = \'block\';\n                            } else {\n                                card.style.display = \'none\';\n                            }\n                        } else {\n                            if (card.dataset.brand === filter) {\n                                card.style.display = \'block\';\n                            } else {\n                                card.style.display = \'none\';\n                            }\n document.querySelector(\'.search-form\');\n            const searchInput = document.querySelector(\'.search-input\');\n            \n            searchForm.addEventListener(\'submit\', function(e) {\n                e.preventDefault();\n                const searchTerm = searchInput.value.trim().toLowerCase();\n                \n                if (searchTerm.length < 2) {\n                    alert(\'Please enter at least 2 characters to search.\');\n                    return;\n                }\n                \n                // Reset filter options\n                filterOptions.forEach(opt => opt.classList.remove(\'active\'));\n                document.querySelector(\'.filter-option[data-filter="all"]\').classList.add(\'active\');\n                \n                // Show/hide superstars based on search\n                let resultsFound = false;\n                superstarCards.forEach(card => {\n                    const superstarName = card.querySelector(\'.superstar-name\').textContent.toLowerCase();\n                    \n                    if (superstarName.includes(searchTerm)) {\n                        card.style.display = \'block\';\n                        resultsFound = true;\n                    } else {\n                        card.style.display = \'none\';\n                    }\n                });\n                \n                if (!resultsFound) {\n                    alert(\'No superstars found matching your search term.\');\n                    // Reset display\n                    superstarCards.forEach(card => {\n                        card.style.display = \'block\';\n                    });\n                }\n            });\n            \n            // Pagination require(\'../models/Superstar\');\nconst Championship = require(\'../models/Championship\');\n\n// Search across all content (superstars, championships)\nexports.searchAll = async (req, res) => {\n  try {\n    const query = req.query.q;\n    \n    if (!query) {\n      return res.status(400).json({ message: \'Search query is required\' });\n    }\n    \n    // Search superstars\n    const superstars = await Superstar.find(\n      { $text: { $search: query } },\n      { score: { $meta: "textScore" } }\n    )\n    .select(\'name nickname brand gender imageUrl thumbnailUrl\')\n    .sort({ score: { $meta: "textScore" } })\n    .limit(10);\n    \n    // Search championships\n    const championships = await Championship.find(\n      { $text: { $search: query } },\n      { score: { $meta: "textScore" } }\n    )\n    .select(\'name type brand imageUrl thumbnailUrl\')\n    .sort({ score: { $meta: "textScore" } })\n    .limit(5);\n    \n    // Combine results\n    const results = {\n      superstars: superstars,\n      championships: championships\n    };\n    \n    res.json(results);\n  } catch (err) {\n    console.error(\'Error searching content:\', err);\n    res.status(500).json({ message: \'Server error\' });\n  }\n};\n\n// Search superstars\nexports.searchSuperstars = async (req, res) => {\n  try {\n    const query = req.query.q;\n    \n    if (!query) {\n      return res.status(400).json({ message: \'Search query is required\' });\n    }\n    \n    // Search superstars\n    const superstars = await Superstar.find(\n      { $text: { $search: query } },\n      { score: { $meta: "textScore" } }\n    )\n    .select(\'name nickname brand gender imageUrl thumbnailUrl\')\n    .sort({ score: { $meta: "textScore" } })\n    .limit(20);\n    \n    res.json(superstars);\n  } catch (err) {\n    console.error(\'Error searching superstars:\', err);\n    res.status(500).json({ message: \'Server error\' });\n  }\n};\n\n// Search championships\nexports.searchChampionships = async (req, res) => {\n  try {\n    const query = req.query.q;\n    \n    if (!query) {\n      return res.status(400).json({ message: \'Search query is required\' });\n    }\n    \n    // Search championships\n    const championships = await Championship.find(\n      { $text: { $search: query } },\n      { score: { $meta: "textScore" } }\n    )\n    .select(\'name type brand imageUrl thumbnailUrl\')\n    .sort({ score: { $meta: "textScore" } })\n    .limit(10);\n    \n    res.json(championships);\n  } catch (err) {\n    console.error(\'Error searching championships:\', err);\n    res.status(500).json({ message: \'Server error\' });\n  }\n};\n\n// Advanced search with filters\nexports.advancedSearch = async (req, res) => {\n  try {\n    const { query, filters } = req.body;\n    \n    if (!query && !filters) {\n      return res.status(400).json({ message: \'Search query or filters are required\' });\n    }\n    \n    let searchQuery = {};\n    \n    // Add text search if query is provided\n    if (query) {\n      searchQuery.$text = { $search: query };\n    }\n    \n    // Add filters if provided\n    if (filters) {\n      // Brand filter\n      if (filters.brand) {\n        searchQuery.brand = filters.brand;\n      }\n      \n      // Gender filter\n      if (filters.gender) {\n        searchQuery.gender = filters.gender;\n      }\n      \n      // Championship filter (current champions only)\n      if (filters.isChampion) {\n        searchQuery[\'championships.currentChampion\'] = true;\n      }\n      \n      // Active/inactive filter\n      if (filters.isActive !== undefined) {\n        searchQuery.isActive = filters.isActive;\n      }\n      \n      // Injured filter\n      if (filters.isInjured !== undefined) {\n        searchQuery.isInjured = filters.isInjured;\n      }\n    }\n    \n    // Execute search\n    const superstars = await Superstar.find(searchQuery)\n      .select(\'name nickname brand gender imageUrl thumbnailUrl isActive isInjured\')\n      .sort(query ? { score: { $meta: "textScore" } } : { name: 1 })\n      .limit(50);\n    \n    res.json(superstars);\n  } catch (err) {\n    console.error(\'Error performing advanced search:\', err);\n    res.status(500).json({ message: \'Server error\' });\n  }\n};\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

He began his wrestling career in 2005, working in the independent circuit, most notably with Ring of Honor (ROH) under the name Tyler Black.</p>\n                    <p>Rollins signed with WWE in 2010 and was assigned to their developmental territory Florida Championship Wrestling (FCW), which was later rebranded as NXT. He became the inaugural NXT Champion in 2012, setting the foundation for his successful main roster career.</p>\n                    <p>In 2012, Rollins debuted on the main roster as part of The Shield alongside Roman Reigns and Dean Ambrose (now Jon Moxley in AEW). He has evolved his character multiple times, from "The Architect" during his time with The Authority to "The Monday Night Messiah" and now "The Visionary."</p>\n                    <p>In August 2025, Rollins captured the World Heavyweight Championship at SummerSlam by cashing in his Money in the Bank contract, beginning his current reign as champion.          <h2 class="profile-section-title">Biography</h2>\n                    <p>Cody Garrett Runnels Rhodes was born in Marietta, Georgia on June 30, 1985. He is the son of WWE Hall of Famer Dusty Rhodes and the half-brother of Dustin Rhodes (formerly known as Goldust in WWE).</p>\n                    <p>Cody began his wrestling career in 2006 in Ohio Valley Wrestling (OVW), WWE\'s developmental territory at the time. He made his main roster debut in 2007 and spent nearly a decade with the company, holding multiple championships including the Intercontinental Championship and various tag team titles.</p>\n                    <p>After leaving WWE in 2016, Rhodes became one of the most influential figures in professional wrestling, competing in promotions like Ring of Honor, New Japan Pro Wrestling, and helping to found All Elite Wrestling (AEW) where he served as an Executive Vice President.</p>\n                    <p>In 2022, Rhodes made a shocking return to WWE at WrestleMania 38, establishing himself as one of the company\'s top stars. His journey culminated at WrestleMania XL in 2024, where he defeated Roman Reigns to win the Undisputed WWE Championship, fulfilling his family\'s legacy.</p>\n                    <p>Currently, Rhodes is in his second reign as WWE Champion after recapturing the title at SummerSlam 2025. He is recognized as one of the top stars in WWE and continues to be one of the most popular superstars on the roster.</p>\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="profile-section">\n          <h2 class="profile-section-title">Biography</h2>\n                    <p>Rebecca Quin, better known by her ring name Becky Lynch, was born on January 30, 1987, in Limerick, Ireland. She began her wrestling training at the age of 15 and made her professional debut in 2002, initially performing under the ring name Rebecca Knox.</p>\n                    <p>Lynch spent several years wrestling on the independent circuit in Europe and North America, including stints in promotions like Shimmer Women Athletes. Her career was temporarily halted in 2006 when she suffered a head injury, leading to a hiatus from wrestling for several years.</p>\n                    <p>In 2013, Lynch signed with WWE and was assigned to their developmental territory NXT. She made her main roster debut in 2015 as part of the "Women\'s Revolution" alongside Charlotte Flair and Sasha Banks.</p>\n                    <p>Lynch\'s career reached new heights in 2018 when she adopted "The Man" persona, becoming one of WWE\'s most popular superstars. This led to her headlining WrestleMania 35 in 2019, where she defeated Ronda Rousey and Charlotte Flair to win both the Raw and SmackDown Women\'s Championships.</p>\n                    <p>After taking time off in 2020 for the birth of her daughter, Lynch returned at SummerSlam 2021. She has since remained one of WWE\'s top female superstars, currently holding the Women\'s Intercontinental Championship, which she won at Money in the Bank 2025.</p>\n                </div>\n\n require(\'path\');\nconst { execSync } = require(\'child_process\');\n\n// Get command line arguments\nconst args = process.argv.slice(2);\nif (args.length < 4) {\n  console.error(\'Usage: node update-champion.js "Championship Name" "New Champion Name" "Event Name" "Date"\');\n  process.exit(1);\n}\n\nconst championshipName = args[0];\nconst newChampionName = args[1];\nconst eventName = process.exit(1);\n}\n\n// Find the championship section\nconst championshipRegex = new RegExp(`<h2 class="championship-name">${championshipName}</h2>[\\\\s\\\\S]*?<div class="championship-holder">([\\\\s\\\\S]*?)</div>`, \'i\');\nconst match = championshipsContent.match(championshipRegex);\n\nif (!match) {\n  console.error(`Championship "${championshipName}" not found in the file.`);\n  process.exit(1);\n}\n\n// Create the new champion HTML\nconst championImageFilename = newChampionName.toLowerCase().replace(/\\s+/g, \'-\') + \'.jpg\';\nconst newChampionHTML     <p>Won at ${eventName} (${date})</p>\n                        </div>\n                    </div>`;\n\n// Replace the old champion with the new one\nconst updatedContent = championshipsContent.replace(match[0], `<h2 class="championship-name">${championshipName}</h2>${newChampionHTML}`);\n\n// Write the updated content back to the file\ntry {\n  fs.writeFileSync(championshipsPath, updatedContent);\n  console.log(`Successfully updated ${championshipName} champion to ${newChampionName}`);\n  \n  // Create a reminder for the image\n  console.log(`Don\'t forget to ensure the champion\'s image exists at: assets/images/superstars/${championImageFilename}`);\n  \n  // Also update the homepage if this is a featured championship\n  console.log(\'You may also need to update the homepage if this championship is featured there.\');\n} catch (err) {\n  console.error(\'Error writing file:\', err);\n  process.exit(1);\n}\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

Massachusetts. Before entering professional wrestling, Cena was a collegiate football player at Springfield College and later worked as a bodybuilder and a limousine driver.</p>\n                    <p>Cena began his professional wrestling career in 1999 with Ultimate Pro Wrestling (UPW) under the ring name "The Prototype." He signed with WWE (then WWF) in 2001 and was assigned to their developmental territory Ohio Valley Wrestling (OVW).</p>\n                    <p>He made his WWE main roster debut in June 2002, answering an open challenge by Kurt Angle. Cena initially portrayed a rapper character, which gained popularity and led to his first major push. He won his first singles championship, the United States Championship, at WrestleMania XX in 2004.</p>\n                    <p>Cena\'s rise to the top of WWE began in 2005 when he won his first WWE Championship at WrestleMania 21 by defeating JBL. Over the next decade, he became the face of WWE, headlining numerous pay-per-views and becoming a 16-time world champion, tying Ric Flair\'s record.</p>\n                    <p>Outside of wrestling, Cena has found success as an actor in Hollywood, starring in films such as "The Marine," "Trainwreck," "Bumblebee," "F9," "The Suicide Squad," and "Peacemaker." He is also known for his extensive charity work, particularly with the Make-A-Wish Foundation, where he has granted over 800 wishes, more than any other celebrity.</p>\n                    <p>In recent years, Cena has transitioned to a part-time schedule with WWE due to his Hollywood commitments. However, he still makes occasional appearances, including his most recent run in 2024-2025 where he announced his retirement tour that will conclude at WrestleMania 42 in 2026.</p>\n                    <p>Throughout his career, Cena has been a polarizing figure among wrestling fans, with his character often receiving mixed reactions despite being positioned as the company\'s top babyface. Nevertheless, his impact on professional wrestling and pop culture is undeniable, cementing his legacy as one of the greatest WWE superstars of all time.</p>\n                </div>\n\n <div class="profile-main">\n                <div class="profile-section">\n                    <h2 class="profile-section-title">Biography</h2>\n                    <p>Brock Edward Lesnar was born on July 12, 1977, in Webster, South Dakota. He grew up on a dairy farm and developed his incredible strength through farm work from an early age. Lesnar was a standout amateur wrestler in high school and college, winning the NCAA Division I Heavyweight Championship in 2000 while at the University of Minnesota.</p>\n                    <p>After college, Lesnar signed with WWE (then WWF) in 2000 and was sent to their developmental territory, Ohio Valley Wrestling (OVW). He made his WWE main roster debut in March 2002 and was quickly pushed as "The Next Big Thing." Within six months of his debut, Lesnar won the King of the Ring tournament and went on to defeat The Rock at SummerSlam 2002 to become the youngest WWE Champion at that time at age 25.</p>\n                    <p>Lesnar\'s first WWE run lasted until 2004, during which he had memorable feuds with Kurt Angle, The Undertaker, and Goldberg. He left WWE after WrestleMania XX to pursue a career in the NFL, signing with the Minnesota Vikings. Though he showed impressive athleticism, he was ultimately cut before the regular season began.</p>\n                    <p>After his NFL attempt, Lesnar pursued a career in mixed martial arts, signing with the UFC in 2008. He quickly rose to prominence, defeating Randy Couture to become the UFC Heavyweight Champion in just his fourth professional MMA fight. His UFC career was hampered by diverticulitis, a serious intestinal condition that required surgery and forced him to take time away from competition.</p>\n                    <p>Lesnar made a shocking return to WWE in 2012, the night after WrestleMania 28. Since then, he has been a dominant force, ending The Undertaker\'s undefeated WrestleMania streak in 2014, delivering 16 German suplexes to John Cena at SummerSlam 2014 in what was dubbed "Suplex City," and holding the Universal Championship for a record 504 days from 2017 to 2018.</p>\n                    <p>Throughout his second WWE run, Lesnar has worked a limited schedule, appearing sporadically and wrestling primarily at major pay-per-view events. This has made his appearances feel special and has maintained his aura as a legitimate combat sports athlete and a unique attraction in WWE.</p>\n                    <p>In 2024, Lesnar returned after a brief hiatus and began a program with Gunther, leading to their highly anticipated match at WrestleMania XL, which Gunther won in a critically acclaimed bout. Lesnar has since continued to make sporadic appearances, maintaining his status as one of WWE\'s biggest stars and most legitimate competitors.</p>\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="profile-section">\n                    <h2 class="profile-section-title">Championship History</h2>\n                    <h3>World Championships</h3>\n                    <div The image should:\n\n1. Be named after the superstar with lowercase letters and hyphens (e.g., `roman-reigns.jpg`, `john-cena.jpg`)\n2. Have a 1:1 aspect ratio (square) for consistency\n3. Be cropped to focus on the superstar\'s face and upper body\n4. Have a resolution of at least 300x300 pixels (600x600 recommended)\n5. Be in JPG or PNG format\n\nYou can use the placeholder generator tool to create temporary images:\n\n```bash\nnode tools/generate-placeholder-images.js\n```\n\n## Adding Championship Images\n\nWhen adding championship images, you need two versions:\n\n1. A small icon version for the championship cards (e.g., `wwe-championship.png`)\n2. A full-size version for the championship detail pages (e.g., `wwe-championship-full.jpg`)\n\nThe icon version should:\n- Be transparent PNG\n- Be approximately 64x36 pixels\n- Show just the championship belt face\n\nThe full-size version should:\n- Be high resolution (at least 800x600)\n- Show the entire championship belt\n- Be in JPG format for better compression\n\n## Background Images\n\nThe background images are SVG files that provide the visual styling for the different sections of the website. If you need to modify them:\n\n1. Edit the SVG files directly in a text editor or SVG editor\n2. Keep the same dimensions and general style for consistency\n3.
